  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_56450f34-03c2-498b-9fcd-f7a52a70ffde'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer4075497518485667232">Piper Griffiths wants one thing in life: To become a Consul, a keeper of the peace between humans and daemons. There are three obstacles in her way.<br/><br/>The first is Lyre. Incubus. Hotter than hell and with a wicked streak to match.   <span id="freeText4075497518485667232" style="display:none">Piper Griffiths wants one thing in life: To become a Consul, a keeper of the peace between humans and daemons. There are three obstacles in her way.<br /><br />The first is Lyre. Incubus. Hotter than hell and with a wicked streak to match. His greatest mission in life is to get Piper into bed and otherwise annoy the crap out of her. The second is Ash. Draconian. Powerful. Dangerous. He knows too much and reveals nothing. Also, disturbingly attractive — and scary. Did she mention scary?<br /><br />The third is the Sahar Stone. Top secret magical weapon of mass destruction. Previously hidden in her Consulate until thieves broke in, went on a murder spree, and disappeared with the weapon.<br /><br />And they left Piper to take the fall for their crimes.<br /><br />Now she’s on the run, her dreams of becoming a Consul shattered and every daemon in the city gunning to kill her. She’s dead on her own, but there’s no one she can trust — no one except two entirely untrustworthy daemons ... See problems one and two.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=my-friends-corrupted-my-soul">my-friends-corrupted-my-soul</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=tbr-shelf-says-thank-you">tbr-shelf-says-thank-you</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1608016496" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2204750268627604289"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423050384ra/13581493.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>☠ <b>DNF at 44%</b>. Because juvenile <s>crap</s> literature isn't me.<br/><br/><b>Yeah, yeah, yeah</b>, I know, I just DNFed yet another fascinating masterpiece. BUT. <b>In my defense</b>, I have to say I had no freaking clue this book was freaking YA when I freaking started reading it. So it's <b>not my fault</b> if I DNFed it. I'm innocent as a newborn child here, people. Had I known this was <s>puerile nonsense</s> youthful prose, I would have done the only sensible thing: I would have DNFed it <b>pre-emptively</b>. It would have saved me from lots </span>
  <span id="freeText2204750268627604289" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423050384ra/13581493.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>☠ <b>DNF at 44%</b>. Because juvenile <s>crap</s> literature isn't me.<br><br><b>Yeah, yeah, yeah</b>, I know, I just DNFed yet another fascinating masterpiece. BUT. <b>In my defense</b>, I have to say I had no freaking clue this book was freaking YA when I freaking started reading it. So it's <b>not my fault</b> if I DNFed it. I'm innocent as a newborn child here, people. Had I known this was <s>puerile nonsense</s> youthful prose, I would have done the only sensible thing: I would have DNFed it <b>pre-emptively</b>. It would have saved me from lots of unnecessary suffering and stuff. <br><br><b>By the way</b>, I would like to take this opportunity to point out that, despite my ♛ queen of DNF ♛ reputation in these parts, a-girl-I-shall-not-name-because-she's-my-friend-and-I-don't-spill <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[don't worry, Shelly, your anonymity is safe with me <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> is <b>much, much worse</b> than my little self in this department. She's devious and cunning so people don't suspect a thing, but believe me, my DNF graveyard is nothing compared to hers. <b>So there</b>.<br><br><b>Okay</b>. Now that we've established I'm a not-so-serial DNFer against my will, let's do the <b>CNR™</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Crappy Non Review, remember? Please do try to follow once in a while, it would make my life much easier. Thank you. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <b>thing</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467279183ra/19573163.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Don't ask me what this cat is doing here, I have no idea.</i><br><br><b>So. Why did I DNF this infantile PoC™</b>? ← don't know what PoC™ means? Too bad. If you read my Delightfully Fascinating Reviews (DFR™) more often, you would know that this is one of my mostest favouritest acronyms ever. But you don't, so you don't. <b>Ha</b>.<br><br>Anyway.<br><br>➽ <b>I DNFed this Infantile PoC™ (IPoC™) because</b>:<br><br>① <b>It's YA</b>. I already said that? Are you sure? Like really, really sure and stuff? Oh well.<br><br>② <b>Me lurrrve me yummy, demons</b> and me <s>want to viciously murder</s> not like immature, silly demons. My dear Annette Marie, may I suggest a <b>How to Write the Mostest Awesomest Demons Ever</b> class by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7277852.Pippa_DaCosta" rel="nofollow noopener">Professor DaCosta</a>? Come to think of it, that might be a bit too complex for you to start with. So I'd suggest signing up for a <b>Demons 101</b> class by Professor <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4721318.S_M_Reine" rel="nofollow noopener">Reine</a> first. Start with the basics and all that. <b>You're welcome</b>. <br><br>③ <b>What's worse than a Love Triangle of Doom and Destruction</b> (LToDaD™)? A YA Triangle of Doom and Destruction (YALToDaD™), obviously. This really is a <b>dream come true</b>. I've always had a soft spot for LToDaDs™, but throw in a YALToDaD™, and I'm seriously doomed. <b>This really here pure bliss</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467100823ra/19550989.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>④ <b>Piper</b>, the enchanting (if slightly underage) heroine, is <b>deliciously TSTL</b>. She sometimes acts like a <b>total nitwit</b>, too. And her character is flatter than a cardboard box. So many endearing qualities. <b>It's beautiful</b>.<br><br>⑤ <b>Ash and Lyre</b>. The deliciously juvenile male demons in residence. <b>Such SUPER HAWT pieces of puerile ass</b>. YUM. I've been waiting for these guys all my life. Damn right I have. Let me tell you, <s>my hot-as-hell sex slaves</s> the guys in my harem are nothing but <b>meaningless little bugs</b> compared to these two. Yep, that's right. Ash and Lyre literally <b>ooooooze hotness and awesomeness and stuff</b>. Oh, and they're <b>SUPER UBER BADDASS AND DANGEROUS</b>, too. I think. Well that's what our lovely <s>and slightly youngish</s> heroine repeats over and over again, so I guess it must be true. <b>Right</b>.<br><br>⑥ <b>Everything</b> in this story is either <b>stereotyped, clichéd, banal</b> or <b>predictable</b>. But it's not ALL bad. Oh no. Sometimes the story is simply <b>badly written</b>. And most times the pace is <b>uneven as hell</b>, too. How delightful. Reading this book decidedly is a <b>glorious experience</b>. <br><br>» <b>And the moral of this CNR™ is</b>: don't read this thing. Well okay, you can read it if you're slightly insane and like YA, but otherwise, don't. This is <b>lethally youthful and deadly crappy stuff</b>. And therefore highly hazardous to your health. <b>Don't say I didn't warn you</b>. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2204750268627604289" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2516763352?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vanessa ♛Queen Alchemy ϟ Novel Nerd Faction♛" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vanessa ♛Queen Alchemy ϟ Novel Nerd Faction♛" href="/user/show/1939326-vanessa-queen-alchemy-novel-nerd-faction">Vanessa ♛Queen Alchemy ϟ Novel Nerd Faction♛</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34727443-chase-the-dark">review of another edition</a>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2516763352" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8025012323352293557">09/17/2020: Reread. (Audiobook.)<br/>08/29/2020: Reread. (Audiobook!)<br/>08/20/2020: Reread! (Read to my son, Maddox.)<br/>07/21/2020: Reread!<br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[I can't even describe how much joy this series brings me. I feel like this series is imprinted on my soul. These characters mean so much to me. Piper is one of my favorite heroines ever. I love how determined and brave she is. I just connect with her so much. Lyre always brings a smile to my face and Ash checks off all the boxes on my book boyfriend list.</span></span>
  <span id="freeText8025012323352293557" style="display:none">09/17/2020: Reread. (Audiobook.)<br />08/29/2020: Reread. (Audiobook!)<br />08/20/2020: Reread! (Read to my son, Maddox.)<br />07/21/2020: Reread!<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I can't even describe how much joy this series brings me. I feel like this series is imprinted on my soul. These characters mean so much to me. Piper is one of my favorite heroines ever. I love how determined and brave she is. I just connect with her so much. Lyre always brings a smile to my face and Ash checks off all the boxes on my book boyfriend list. These characters are complex and have such insane chemistry with one another. I love the deep friendship that Piper forms with Lyre and Ash that continues to get stronger throughout the series. This series will always be my favorite. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />10/17/2019: Reread!<br />05/13/2019: Reread!<br />02/28/2019: Reread!<br />09/09/2018: Reread!<br />09/02/2018: Reread!<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I literally just finished re-reading this series two days ago and I have already started book one again! I seriously cannot get these characters or this world out of my mind. I never want to leave! Book hangover to the max. I love this series so much it brings me actual physical pain from all the feels. &lt;3 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Simply put this series is brilliant! The premise is exciting and fresh. I really love this unique and clever take on the traditional mythology of the Underworld and Heaven. Of demons and angels and where Earth fits in the middle of them. I love how Marie's take on these is not what anyone would ever expect. Her ideas are entirely original. The world-building is insanely detailed. There are three different worlds that are described vividly. There are different castes of supernatural creatures, called daemons, from both the Overworld and the Underworld, and they all have their different physical features, characteristics, loyalties, and ways of life. There are the offspring of humans and daemons which are referred to as haemons. And then there are the humans. There is a large amount of information surrounding this world, but it is not thrown at the reader to overwhelm them. The world-building is very fluid. It moves with the reader as the story progresses and everything feels natural. No info dumps or mind clutter of too much information. I especially love the blending of genres in this book. This book is urban fantasy, dystopian, paranormal, and supernatural all at once. I love how it doesn't feel like one single genre while reading. It feels apart from a single definition because it represents each of these genres equally well. <br /><br />The characters are as wonderful as I remember. These are some of my all-time favorite characters in a book ever. EVER. They are well written with exciting and compelling character arcs. The chemistry between the characters and the witty dialogue are some of my favorite parts of the book. <br /><br />The plot is exciting and I could not stop reading! The plot has been crafted with precision and it will leave you a lifelong fan of the author. You won't be able to put her books down! <br /><br />The romance in this book is absolutely perfect! It is a slow-burn romance that will leave your heart pumping quickly. The way that the love interests come together is another thing that has been expertly crafted in this book. I don't know of another way to describe how perfectly the romance plays out. It is convincing and so entirely swoon-worthy!<br /><br />Overall, loved reading this again! I had the immediate urge to read it again after finishing the series for the second time. This is a book series that I will continue to reread and enjoy. If you haven't tried an Annette Marie book then you are missing out on a pot of gold at the end of the rainbow. <br /><br />ORIGINAL REVIEW<br />Okay, I now have a new favorite series and a new favorite author!! I cannot stress enough how absolutely amazing this book is! This book surpassed all of my expectations and then some. It has everything that I love about young adult books. I simply could not stop reading.<br /><br />What I liked<br />These characters are perfection! I instantly fell in love with the three main characters in this series. They are magical. And the way that they flow off of one another's chemistry is flawless. <br /><br />The character development is amazing! The backstories and the little things that make up who a character really is shine through. I felt like I knew these characters on a personal level. I felt what they felt and experienced things with them. I just felt so close to them.<br /><br />While this story is based on other popular ideas, the way that Annette Marie fashioned it is wholly unique. I have never read anything like it. I loved the world that Annette Marie created in this book. I was devouring every detail and I couldn't get enough!<br /><br />The plot is catching and well thought out. The whole story flows so nicely. There are twists and turns to keep you guessing. All of the elements of a great story are perfectly balanced to keep you wanting more and more. <br /><br />I loved the writing style. The story is written very fluidly, taking you exactly where you need to go at exactly the right time. It's brilliant.<br /><br />What I didn't like<br />Thinking the series over in my head, I can't come up with a single thing that I disliked while I was reading this series. Not a thing. Seriously. I think that only thing that I dislike is that it comes to an end. <br /><br />Would I Recommend It<br />YES, OMG, YES!!! Get. This. Series. NOW!! If you pick up this series you will not be disappointed. It is rare that a book or a book series touches me so deeply, but this one has become my new favorite. I haven't felt this passionate about a book series in a long time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8025012323352293557" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1174425984" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1174425984" />
    <a title="Sophia Sardothien" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28997068-sophia-sardothien"><img alt="Sophia Sardothien" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1418655691p2/28997068.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1174425984?book_show_action=true">Jan 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Sardothien" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Sardothien" href="/user/show/28997068-sophia-sardothien">Sophia Sardothien</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23367203-chase-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1174425984" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1736882209991877972">This book is fun, dangerous, action-packed, page-turner and anything a good urban fantasy should be. The word building in this book is unique and alluring. Seventy years ago, daemons put an end to humanity’s third world war to prevent the destruction of their favorite playground, Earth. So now humans are to live a degraded life, where the consul are to remain the peace between humans and daemons. Our main female lead Piper Griffiths is the daughter of the head consul, for her entire life she onl</span>
  <span id="freeText1736882209991877972" style="display:none">This book is fun, dangerous, action-packed, page-turner and anything a good urban fantasy should be. The word building in this book is unique and alluring. Seventy years ago, daemons put an end to humanity’s third world war to prevent the destruction of their favorite playground, Earth. So now humans are to live a degraded life, where the consul are to remain the peace between humans and daemons. Our main female lead Piper Griffiths is the daughter of the head consul, for her entire life she only wants one thing; to become a Consul. However as usual shit happens, with the help of two sexy daemons she has to save the world (well you know what happens) <br /><br />I really did like the world the author builded up, it was really different and idiosyncratic in paranormal // urban fantasy standards, the author did not just created another world with daemons but one that has so much more extent. However it would be so much better if all the details are not forced together all at once, the author could have taken more time describing the amazing world she came up with rather then putting it all together all at once creating a immense confusion. <br /><br />The other thing I really enjoy about the book is the characters, meanwhile Piper our main female lead is really naïve and from times to times unreasonably stubborn and impulsive. But she definitely is a likeable protagonist whom is a good fighter and unlike typical paranormal romances protagonists Piper has a certain depth that held in her that captivated me into reading in her perspective. As for the other two other male leads Lyre and Ash, both are incredibly sexy and swoonworthy male leads. They are incredible, while Lyre is hot and fierce Ash is all powerful and dangerous, the author has successfully compluse me into falling in love with both of them. I won't say there is a absoulte love triangle happening despite the synopsis, as it is clear to Piper when it is just "lust" or real "love" happening. Which I extremely appreciate the different path the author took <br /><br />I really would like to say more of this book as it was an extremely entertaining read, in some ways this book reminded me of sweet evil but for the most part it is a lot more different, :D highly recommend if you are looking for GREAT paranormal romances :) SERIOUSLY THIS BOOK DESERVE SO MUCH MORE RECOGNITION!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1736882209991877972" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2097561476" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2097561476" />
    <a title="✶Rachelle✶ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26462337-rachelle"><img alt="✶Rachelle✶ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514745698p2/26462337.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39023148-annika?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39023148-annika?shelf=favorite-serials">favorite-serials</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39023148-annika?shelf=love-love-love">love-love-love</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1212030637" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16730380416274503901"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453375073i/17818103.jpg' width='130' height='30' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>First read: 03/2016 - 5 stars<br/>Second read: 01/2020 - still 5 stars!</i><br/><br/><br/>Being the only haemon (half human, half daemon) in existence without any magical powers isn't easy. Frowned upon by humans and not seen as an equal by either haemons or daemons, Piper is used to having to prove herself to everyone. Little does she know that what starts out as a harmless job of "babysitting" two daemons will eventually become her biggest test so far.<br/>Now stuck with a perpetually horny incubus and a dark and dangerou</span>
  <span id="freeText16730380416274503901" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453375073i/17818103.jpg" width="130" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>First read: 03/2016 - 5 stars<br>Second read: 01/2020 - still 5 stars!</i><br><br><br>Being the only haemon (half human, half daemon) in existence without any magical powers isn't easy. Frowned upon by humans and not seen as an equal by either haemons or daemons, Piper is used to having to prove herself to everyone. Little does she know that what starts out as a harmless job of "babysitting" two daemons will eventually become her biggest test so far.<br>Now stuck with a perpetually horny incubus and a dark and dangerous draconian, Piper finds herself on the run from the most powerful of daemons, some pissed off humans and even a political organization that has nothing to lose.<br><br>Oh, this was amazing!<br>I can't say it often enough: I freaking love bad-ass heroines, especially in the Paranormal/ Urban Fantasy genre. And that is exactly what Piper is. Funny, smart, quick-witted, and most importantly, she totally kicks ass - with her three black belts in martial arts, her iron will and her incorruptible sense of justice. The novel is told completely from her POV and I thoroughly enjoyed being in that quick mind of hers.<br>Her two sidekicks, Lyre and Ash, were amazing additions, too. I instantly fell in love with them the moment I "met" them, Lyre being this delicious, flirty, tongue-in-cheek incubus you just can't help but like, while Ash is his total opposite: dark, brooding and lethal.<br><i>
  <blockquote>She closed her eyes. The only two people in the world she could trust right now were sitting on either side of her and she couldn't trust them at all.</blockquote>
</i><br>Love triangle? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Update after reading the entire series: absolutely <b>no</b> love triangle, even if it may seem like it at the beginning. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This book was a fast-paced, non-stop action ride from start to finish with some fantastic world-building, partly dystopian but mainly Urban Fantasy, unexpected twists lurking at every turn, and a wide array of intriguing and inscrutable characters.<br>The only regret I have is not having started this series way earlier, even though <i>Chase the Dark</i> has been on my TBR list since forever.<br><br><i>ARC provided by the publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16730380416274503901" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13421497436773811606">*revised review (more focused on the series as a whole) below the three wiggly dashes!*<br/><br/>buddy read with the wonderful Diana! <br/><br/>oh my god i missed Annette Marie's writing! it's crazy addictive and i can never put her books down, and i both love and hate Annette for that. Chase the Dark was no exception! with a badass MC, a flirty but sweet incubus, a sexy scary dragon dude and an adorable little (sometimes) dragon pet thing, i loved this story. the characters were amazing, the action and storyline w</span>
  <span id="freeText13421497436773811606" style="display:none">*revised review (more focused on the series as a whole) below the three wiggly dashes!*<br /><br />buddy read with the wonderful Diana! <br /><br />oh my god i missed Annette Marie's writing! it's crazy addictive and i can never put her books down, and i both love and hate Annette for that. Chase the Dark was no exception! with a badass MC, a flirty but sweet incubus, a sexy scary dragon dude and an adorable little (sometimes) dragon pet thing, i loved this story. the characters were amazing, the action and storyline was impeccable, and the romance left me craving more. ugh, Ash is just.... everything (he's right up there with Zylas and Shiro and i love it). <br /><br />onto the next book!!<br /><br />~~~<br /><br />i considered writing an actual review down here but.... i don't know if i can be bothered.<br />basically this was a fun and entertaining series (apart from that ending) with characters that i fell in love with, and Annette Marie's iconic addictive writing that you can't put down. our little cheese-loving Zwi was a darling and a half (you get more Zwi in the collection of scenes in Lyre and Ash's POV) and Lyre was much more 3D and interesting than i originally thought. Ash and Piper both had amazing character development throughout the series, and their relationship definitely grew and improved as the series continued, which i loved. also Kiev! i highkey loved him, what a cutie!<br />all up, this was a good series, just not as amazing as Red Winter (god i miss Shiro... everyone should read Red Winter pronto) or Guild Codex: Demonized (everyone should also read Taming Demons for Beginners ASAP. Zylas.... now that's a demon i would love to meet).<br />still, this was a fun buddy read! thanks Diana hon!<br />(yep, this is the same series review that i posted for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35238331.Unleash_the_Storm__Steel___Stone___5_" title="Unleash the Storm (Steel &amp; Stone, #5) by Annette Marie" rel="nofollow noopener">Unleash the Storm</a>. ah well, deal with it.)</span>

<div id="review_1190865132" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1190865132" />
    <a title="Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32873228-nicole"><img alt="Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1418215014p2/32873228.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1190865132?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nicole" href="/user/show/32873228-nicole">Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1190865132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2535633497940433670">WTF even was this book? The plot made no sense and the number of typos or missing words was extremely distracting. Major plot points are missing (what even IS the Sahar?), the dialogue is often nonsensical, and moments that do nothing to move the plot forward (i.e. the fight in the club) are drawn out ad nauseam. The book also tries to beat you over the head with sex, but in a very obvious, trying-too-hard sort of way - rather than the characters acting sexy, the reader is told (repeatedly) that</span>
  <span id="freeText2535633497940433670" style="display:none">WTF even was this book? The plot made no sense and the number of typos or missing words was extremely distracting. Major plot points are missing (what even IS the Sahar?), the dialogue is often nonsensical, and moments that do nothing to move the plot forward (i.e. the fight in the club) are drawn out ad nauseam. The book also tries to beat you over the head with sex, but in a very obvious, trying-too-hard sort of way - rather than the characters acting sexy, the reader is told (repeatedly) that they are sexy but with nothing to substantiate it. Zwi is obviously just a smaller version of Toothless from How to Train Your Dragon, which is cute, but borders on character theft. The writing is too juvenile for teens and just plain insulting for adults. I have no idea why this is so highly rated by other Goodreaders, who are usually spot on. DO NOT READ.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2535633497940433670" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2490015353" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2490015353" />
    <a title="nuin giliath" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69607555-nuin-giliath"><img alt="nuin giliath" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595720802p2/69607555.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2490015353?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="nuin giliath" class="user" itemprop="url" name="nuin giliath" href="/user/show/69607555-nuin-giliath">nuin giliath</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34727443-chase-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69607555-nuin-giliath?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69607555-nuin-giliath?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69607555-nuin-giliath?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69607555-nuin-giliath?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2490015353" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14411959430354389417"><b>Final rating: 3.5/5</b><br/><br/>I went into this book with little to no expectations and I'm really glad I did. With this being the first installment in a multi-book series, a significant amount of time was spent on world-building and establishing characters/relationships. Sometimes I felt bogged down with the amount of information provided, yet I see a lot of potential here in regards to the story that the author is trying to tell over the course of this series. <br/><br/>At times, I thought the plot progressed rathe</span>
  <span id="freeText14411959430354389417" style="display:none"><b>Final rating: 3.5/5</b><br /><br />I went into this book with little to no expectations and I'm really glad I did. With this being the first installment in a multi-book series, a significant amount of time was spent on world-building and establishing characters/relationships. Sometimes I felt bogged down with the amount of information provided, yet I see a lot of potential here in regards to the story that the author is trying to tell over the course of this series. <br /><br />At times, I thought the plot progressed rather slowly, but thankfully there were frequent action scenes which helped to move things along and recapture my interest. While some aspects were rather convenient and predictable, some of the twists/reveals did take me by surprise which increased my overall enjoyment.<br /><br />I admit that I wasn't a huge fan of the characters at first, however they really grew on me by the end. Yes, Piper was impulsive and sometimes a bit immature, but I liked how her lack of magical abilities caused her to develop and rely on her own physical strength, fighting skills, and a knowledge of the daemon world. When I first encountered her daemon companions, I figured they'd be stereotypical YA male leads/love interests, but I actually found them to be more complex and intriguing than I anticipated.<br /><br />While this wasn't particularly moving or deep, it was a fun adventure and I enjoyed the time I spent reading it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14411959430354389417" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42319420-lonna-flyl-f?shelf=2015-challenge">2015-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1327811308" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12958944779607122403"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432224148i/14910585.png' alt='FLYLeF Book Reviews' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Original Post: <a href='http://reviews.flylef.com/2015/08/chase-the-dark.html' target='_new' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <em>Chase the Dark</em>
</a> at <a href='http://www.flylef.com/' target='_new' rel='nofollow noopener'>FLYLeF</a> (<a href='http://www.flylef.com/' target='_new' rel='nofollow noopener'>www.flylef.com</a>)<br/><br/><em>CHASE THE DARK</em>, by Annette Marie, is a very promising start to the Steel and Stone series – a young adult contemporary fantasy. It’s a light and fun read. But where it lacks in heftiness, it more than makes up with the intriguing characters and their nearly impossible undertakings.<br/><br/>Meet Piperel Griffiths – half human, half daemon – a haeman. All Piper ever wanted was to become a Consul, a keeper of peace between humans and daemons. Life </span>
  <span id="freeText12958944779607122403" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432224148i/14910585.png" alt="FLYLeF Book Reviews" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Original Post: <a href="http://reviews.flylef.com/2015/08/chase-the-dark.html" target="_new" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <em>Chase the Dark</em>
</a> at <a href="http://www.flylef.com/" target="_new" rel="nofollow noopener">FLYLeF</a> (<a href="http://www.flylef.com/" target="_new" rel="nofollow noopener">www.flylef.com</a>)<br><br><em>CHASE THE DARK</em>, by Annette Marie, is a very promising start to the Steel and Stone series – a young adult contemporary fantasy. It’s a light and fun read. But where it lacks in heftiness, it more than makes up with the intriguing characters and their nearly impossible undertakings.<br><br>Meet Piperel Griffiths – half human, half daemon – a haeman. All Piper ever wanted was to become a Consul, a keeper of peace between humans and daemons. Life as the daughter of the powerful Head Consul was surprisingly uneventful: school, training, and homework. That is until the “sinfully irresistible” Lyre, the “enigmatic and lethal” Ash, and the destructive Sahar Stone converge in an explosive way snapping her out of her reverie. Framed for stealing the Stone, she runs for her life with only Lyre and Ash to aid her. She embarks on a deadly quest to clear her name and quite possibly loose her heart.<br><br><em>Chase the Dark</em> definitely tilts the scale more towards contemporary fantasy than paranormal romance...for now. But, romance fans will be rewarded with their patience as a delicious love story slowly unravels. It’s not instantaneous and wild, but rather slow and sweet – like unexpectedly falling in love with your best friend. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12958944779607122403" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090036546" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1090036546?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="CasPerfitz~SLiTsReaD" class="user" itemprop="url" name="CasPerfitz~SLiTsReaD" href="/user/show/9406114-casperfitz-slitsread">CasPerfitz~SLiTsReaD</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1090036546" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10418549808965902700">#Paranormal #UrbanFantasy #ComingOfAge #Magical<br/><br/>I loved this!!!! <br/><br/>We got two sexy daemon heroes. First, there’s Lyre an Incubus who is “hotter than hell”, he has a fun and flirtatious personality and loves to constantly tease Piper. Then there’s Ash, a Draconian. He is powerful, dangerous and scary. Personality wise, he is the exact opposite of Lyre. Both makes the perfect heroes. But yes, I do love one of them more :D… I am a sucker for powerful and intense alpha. And Ash pretty much falls into t</span>
  <span id="freeText10418549808965902700" style="display:none">#Paranormal #UrbanFantasy #ComingOfAge #Magical<br /><br />I loved this!!!! <br /><br />We got two sexy daemon heroes. First, there’s Lyre an Incubus who is “hotter than hell”, he has a fun and flirtatious personality and loves to constantly tease Piper. Then there’s Ash, a Draconian. He is powerful, dangerous and scary. Personality wise, he is the exact opposite of Lyre. Both makes the perfect heroes. But yes, I do love one of them more :D… I am a sucker for powerful and intense alpha. And Ash pretty much falls into that category. ;)<br /><br />Now the heroine, Piper, a Haemon, meaning she is half human, half daemon. She also has a quite loveable character. She is sweet and although she lacks magic, she can kick ass! Her sole purpose is to become a Consul, a keeper of the peace between humans and daemons, and make her father proud, who happens to be the head of the Consulate. <br /><br />But when someone went to steal the Sahar Stone, a top secret magical weapon of mass destruction, leaving behind bodies of dead people… Piper was left to take the fall for the crime.<br /><br />So now, Piper is on the run with no one to trust except the two daemon, Lyre and Ash. But could she trust them?<br /><br />This is a fast paced, heart pumping action packed book. Given there is no romance involved (yet), it is high on sexual tension! And with just the right amount of humour. <br /><br />It didn’t take long for me to be drawn in the story. It comes with a lot of surprising twists. It is magical, we got all sorts of daemons and underworld creatures… And great world building. <br /><br />Since this is just the start of a series, the ending left me desperate for the next book… which is already out for pre-order in <a>Amazon</a>. And, incidentally, the first book is free for kindle unlimited subscribers.<br /><br />Ms. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8546572.Annette_Marie" title="Annette Marie" rel="nofollow noopener">Annette Marie</a> is definitely going up on my list of authors to watch for. <br /><br />One of my favourite scenes were when Piper, in exchanged for an information they needed, ended up in the fight ring. A no-holds-barred fight... with daemons... Not to the death, but the fighters will not stop until someone is beaten unconscious. It is a must-read. I wanted to copy that scene here but considering I think it is one of the highlight of the story, I should refrain from doing so. :D</span>
  <a data-text-id="10418549808965902700" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1315204096" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1315204096" />
    <a title="Kristen Burns" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/42225826-kristen-burns"><img alt="Kristen Burns" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1436601871p2/42225826.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1315204096?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen Burns" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen Burns" href="/user/show/42225826-kristen-burns">Kristen Burns</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=fave-male-character">fave-male-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=beautiful-writing">beautiful-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=dragons">dragons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=paranormal-urban-fantasy">paranormal-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=read-2015-books">read-2015-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=fave-side-character">fave-side-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1315204096" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5653657151849445442">5 Stars<br/><br/>I. Love. This. Book.<br/><br/>$%#@&!!!<br/><br/>That was what my brain was doing the whole time I was reading.<br/><br/>So where do I even start?!<br/><br/>First, the characters. All three main characters were great. Lyre was flirty and playful but also ridiculously lovable and kind. Ash was mysterious and dangerous but also loyal and protective. Piper was kickass and intelligent but also emotionally vulnerable and forgiving. They were three-dimensional, all unique from each other, and it made for a really interesting team and </span>
  <span id="freeText5653657151849445442" style="display:none">5 Stars<br /><br />I. Love. This. Book.<br /><br />$%#@&amp;!!!<br /><br />That was what my brain was doing the whole time I was reading.<br /><br />So where do I even start?!<br /><br />First, the characters. All three main characters were great. Lyre was flirty and playful but also ridiculously lovable and kind. Ash was mysterious and dangerous but also loyal and protective. Piper was kickass and intelligent but also emotionally vulnerable and forgiving. They were three-dimensional, all unique from each other, and it made for a really interesting team and dynamic between characters. I also loved, loved, LOVED Ash's daemon form and the way the whole concept of shading played into the story. Ok, I really just loved everything about Ash and his terrifying, brooding, dangerous, yet so-full-of-goodness ways, but I'll let you get to know him yourself!<br /><br />And the plot? PERFECT! It flowed so organically, never forced. The obstacles and problems that continued to spring up were not sheer coincidence or the outcome of ridiculous, too-stupid-to-live decisions. Also, there was a clear goal from the beginning, something I love because I like to know where my stories are headed instead of feeling like I'm aimlessly wandering. To top it all off, it completely engaged me to the point that I was clutching at my shirt, pausing at certain parts just to take a breath, and laughing out loud.<br /><br />And the writing style! I have to talk about the writing style because I was so in love. I'm big on the whole highlighting thing when I read on my kindle, but I found myself wanting to highlight entire pages because it was all so beautifully written that I couldn't even choose one line or figure out where to stop.<br /><br />Also, technically, this book is YA, but I didn't get that stereotypical YA vibe at all. Piper was actually mature with the ability to make GOOD decisions and to not sit around being self-deprecating the way characters often do in YA.<br /><br />My review has gotten ridiculously long, and this book is never going to live up to anyone's expectations after reading this, but I just loved it too much to rein in my excitement. I didn't even hesitate to immediately buy an ebook copy after renting it from Amazon Prime and then the paperback later on.<br /><br />I think on some subconscious level I've made it my personal mission in life to make this series more well-known because I recommend it every chance I get, even to strangers. This was an unbelievably amazing start to a series that I recommend to everyone who likes fantasy (and maybe even those who don't)!<br /><br /><a href="http://blog.kristenburns.com/book-review-chase-the-dark-by-annette-marie/" rel="nofollow noopener">Original Review on Blog</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="5653657151849445442" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2138812520" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2138812520" />
    <a title="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog"><img alt="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576986930p2/28353412.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2138812520?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" href="/user/show/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog">Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34727443-chase-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=bad-boys-i-love">bad-boys-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=creatures-demons">creatures-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=dont-cry">dont-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=sigh-bbf">sigh-bbf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=favorite-heroines">favorite-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2138812520" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer39231410177784283"><b>
  <i>Buddy Read with Sophie at <a href='https://bewareofthereader.com/chase-the-dark-by-annette-marie-review-of-a-buddy-read-and-addictive-series/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beware of the Reader</a> and Raven at <a href='https://dreamyaddictions.wordpress.com/category/blog/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Dreamy Addictions</a></i>
</b><br/><br/>Chase The Dark was an action packed ride that had me completely obsessed. <strong>With magic, secrets, friendship, betrayal, lust and the beginnings of something more in the pages, I fell madly in love with this book.</strong> The characters became my friends and not only did I deeply feel everything they did, but I was terrified with what was to come next. There was a richness to the world they lived in, and I felt like I was with </span>
  <span id="freeText39231410177784283" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Buddy Read with Sophie at <a href="https://bewareofthereader.com/chase-the-dark-by-annette-marie-review-of-a-buddy-read-and-addictive-series/" rel="nofollow noopener">Beware of the Reader</a> and Raven at <a href="https://dreamyaddictions.wordpress.com/category/blog/" rel="nofollow noopener">Dreamy Addictions</a></i>
</b><br><br>Chase The Dark was an action packed ride that had me completely obsessed. <strong>With magic, secrets, friendship, betrayal, lust and the beginnings of something more in the pages, I fell madly in love with this book.</strong> The characters became my friends and not only did I deeply feel everything they did, but I was terrified with what was to come next. There was a richness to the world they lived in, and I felt like I was with them every step of the way. If you love urban fantasy, friendships, action or slow burn romance then definitely add this one to your tbr!<br><blockquote>
  
    <strong>The only two people in the world she could trust right now were sitting on either side of her and she couldn’t trust them at all. They were daemons.</strong>
  
</blockquote><br><strong>By that second page, I already loved Piper Griffiths' thoughts. </strong>She was an Apprentice Consul and worked and lived at the Consulate, which was like an embassy to the daemons. Our world had been opened to the Underworld and Overworld years ago and the Consuls helped keep the peace and protected humans from daemons. Right from the beginning we got to see Piper's fighting skills. <strong>She was fierce, deadly and totally kicked ass. </strong>Piper was a haemon, part human and daemon, but she possessed no magic like the other haemons and daemons around her. And that was a huge issue, since all Consul's had magic to help keep the peace.<br><blockquote>
  
    <strong>Some nights she wondered if she was looking for goodness in him that wasn’t there. Other nights, she imagined a thousand ways to tell him thank you and none seemed good enough.</strong>
  
</blockquote><br>While daemons stayed at the Consulate, there were two she'd seen around before. Lyre and Ash. <strong>Lyre was an incubus, who was sexy, playful, intoxicating and fun. </strong>He had a heart of gold underneath it all and I loved watching how much he cared for his friends. And then there was Ash. He was a draconian who was extremely powerful and had a dangerous reputation. Others feared and respected him, so I was leery of him, just like Piper. But when Piper got framed for taking the Sahar Stone, a magical weapon of mass destruction, she found herself running for her life. With Lyre and Ash right by her side.<br><blockquote>
  
    <strong>The world was spinning but Ash’s arms were steady and strong. Always strong. He was her only rock in the ocean of adversity that had flooded her life since the night of the attack on the Consulate. He was the only one who showed up again and again, his strength offered, nothing asked in return.</strong>
  
</blockquote><br>While I loved Lyre, <strong>I found myself becoming obsessed with Ash. </strong>Ash was a huge mystery who was sarcastic, smart, and quick on his feet. <strong>He was so subtle and mysterious that he pulled me right into his dark web.</strong> Especially since he helped defend and protect Piper's life every step of the way, even if they struggled or butted heads with each other. And the moments where he would show his emotions, <em>oh</em>, Ash stole my breath away.<br><blockquote>
  
    <strong>She clamped her fingers over the back of his head and pulled him closer still, demanding even more. His hand tightened in her hair and she tilted her head farther back as their kiss deepened into something even wilder.</strong>
  
</blockquote><br>Ash, Lyre and Piper were running for their lives, while trying to prove their innocence. Being thrown into life and death situations made them quickly form a bond and I loved how much they trusted each other. Moments between them made me smile and laugh, which was needed with all of the action that surrounded them. It felt like I always had sweaty palms lol. On top of that, <strong>I had <em>no</em> clue what was going to happen next. Just like that moment with the hottest kiss ever *fans face*. Yup I was obsessed.</strong><br><blockquote>
  
    <strong>Black irises met hers. Terror sucked out the breath she’d just taken. She clenched her teeth and fought to remember his careful touch on her cheek. He wouldn’t hurt her. He wouldn’t. He’d promised.</strong>
  
</blockquote><br><strong>Chase the Dark was impossible to put down! </strong> And while I figured out one thing, there were quite a few twists I didn't see coming. So with betrayal, secrets, friendship, lies, and trust, you can count on this book pulling your emotions every which way. Plus I have<em> so </em>much hope for a certain two characters. If they move forward, their love for each other is going to be beyond powerful *fingers crossed*!<br><blockquote>
  
    <strong>“Is he alive, Zwi?” she whispered. She gathered the little creature against her chest and hugged her gently. “Please let him be alive.”</strong>
  
</blockquote><br>PS I don't want to say how she's connected to the story, but I loved Zwi with my whole heart. She was a little dragonet, and I wanted to steal her out of this book!<br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i> <br><a title="Star-Crossed Book Blog" href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1516600667i/24898353._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b> </b>
</u><br><a title="Instagram" href="https://www.instagram.com/starcrossedbookblog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1981676577" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1981676577" />
    <a title="Di" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21177980-di"><img alt="Di" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467113283p2/21177980.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1981676577?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Di" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Di" href="/user/show/21177980-di">Di</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34727443-chase-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21177980-di?shelf=feeding-my-ya-addiction">feeding-my-ya-addiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21177980-di?shelf=favourite-authors">favourite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21177980-di?shelf=series-i-loved">series-i-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21177980-di?shelf=rereads">rereads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21177980-di?shelf=some-of-the-reasons-i-love-ya-books">some-of-the-reasons-i-love-ya-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21177980-di?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21177980-di?shelf=wish-list">wish-list</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1981676577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14820318200496563585">This book was a really fun ride. It's been sooo long since I've read a good YA Urban Fantasy and this one was a serious page turner. It's action packed, engaging, funny and unique.<br/><br/>I actually picked this one up as soon as I finished <a href='http://bookreviewsbydi.blogspot.com/2017/10/review-night-realm-annette-marie.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Night Realm</a> and I'm totally HOOKED! <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8546572.Annette_Marie' title='Annette Marie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Annette Marie</a> has just got a way of grabbing my attention and never letting go.<br/><br/><b>I'm a huge fan of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8546572.Annette_Marie' title='Annette Marie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Annette Marie</a>'s heroines and the main character of this one is no exception.</b> <br/><br/>Piper is essentially a haemon (human x daemon) althoug</span>
  <span id="freeText14820318200496563585" style="display:none">This book was a really fun ride. It's been sooo long since I've read a good YA Urban Fantasy and this one was a serious page turner. It's action packed, engaging, funny and unique.<br /><br />I actually picked this one up as soon as I finished <a href="http://bookreviewsbydi.blogspot.com/2017/10/review-night-realm-annette-marie.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Night Realm</a> and I'm totally HOOKED! <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8546572.Annette_Marie" title="Annette Marie" rel="nofollow noopener">Annette Marie</a> has just got a way of grabbing my attention and never letting go.<br /><br /><b>I'm a huge fan of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8546572.Annette_Marie" title="Annette Marie" rel="nofollow noopener">Annette Marie</a>'s heroines and the main character of this one is no exception.</b> <br /><br />Piper is essentially a haemon (human x daemon) although she was born of two haemon parents and she has none of the magical abilities that a haemon born of a human and daemon combo.<br /><br />Even without magic, Piper is a force to be reckoned with and she shows how pure bravery and determination can often be more powerful than brute force. She felt so authentic and just the sort of character that I can relate to and that girls can realistically aspire to be. <br /><br />There are two main male protagonists, Ash and Lyre and I adored them both. <br /><br />Having read <a href="http://bookreviewsbydi.blogspot.com/2017/10/review-night-realm-annette-marie.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Night Realm</a> which follows Lyre I was already completely in love with that incubus. He's flirty and seductive and yet trustworthy and loyal. <br /><br /><blockquote>If sex appeal were an artist, he was its masterpiece.</blockquote><br /><br />Ash is a bad boy, through and through but what red blooded woman wouldn't have a little thing for him? He's powerful, understated and BAD, BAD, BAD. But at the same time he's also fiercely protective, vulnerable and broken and . . . Can you tell I'm #TeamAsh?<br /><br /><blockquote>Unlike Lyre, he didn’t have that cultivated appeal of “I’m a little bad, but you can trust me.” Ash was <i>all</i> bad.<br /></blockquote><br /><br /><b>The chemistry is sizzling off the pages</b> and although there wasn't really a romance to speak of there's definitely <i>something</i> there and I found myself shipping HARD. I've seen some whispers of a love triangle, but I really didn't see it that way. Lyre just can't help being Lyre and whether I'm influenced from reading <a href="http://bookreviewsbydi.blogspot.com/2017/10/review-night-realm-annette-marie.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Night Realm</a> first, I'm not sure... But I'm still saying NO LOVE TRIANGLE. <br /><br />The world building is excellent as usual although there were a few small things that made me think that this might be the author's debut novel. Nothing that really impacted my enjoyment though.<br /><br />The dialogue is so FUN - it made me laugh out loud and I loved the banter and the wit and snark and the dynamic between the team.<br /><br /><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34727443.Chase_the_Dark__Steel___Stone___1_" title="Chase the Dark (Steel &amp; Stone, #1) by Annette Marie" rel="nofollow noopener">Chase the Dark</a> is addictive, fun, fast and extremely entertaining</b> - just my sort of book!<br /><br /><blockquote>Some daemons you can’t help but fear. You will always be afraid. It’s human nature.<br /></blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="14820318200496563585" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1131577656" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1131577656" />
    <a title="Kathylill " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2604354-kathylill"><img alt="Kathylill " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1422885397p2/2604354.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1131577656?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathylill " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathylill " href="/user/show/2604354-kathylill">Kathylill </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2604354-kathylill?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2604354-kathylill?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2604354-kathylill?shelf=wished-more-people-knew-about">wished-more-people-knew-about</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2604354-kathylill?shelf=mouthwatering-alphas-with-scars">mouthwatering-alphas-with-scars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2604354-kathylill?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1131577656" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18028721818460373903">I really liked this book and recommend it to everyone who likes urban fantasy with dark & dangerous demons and scary “angels”. The world building is not really unique but still interesting. After humanity almost wiped itself out during something akin to World War III, the demons from the Underwold (dark) and Overworld (bright) revealed themselves and destroyed all mass destruction weapons thus saving Earth, their favorite playground. Humans now live in a kind of dystopian future, where consul in</span>
  <span id="freeText18028721818460373903" style="display:none">I really liked this book and recommend it to everyone who likes urban fantasy with dark &amp; dangerous demons and scary “angels”. The world building is not really unique but still interesting. After humanity almost wiped itself out during something akin to World War III, the demons from the Underwold (dark) and Overworld (bright) revealed themselves and destroyed all mass destruction weapons thus saving Earth, their favorite playground. Humans now live in a kind of dystopian future, where consul intermediaries (try to) keep the peace between humans and demons from both worlds. I really liked the backstory; I just wish Annette Marie would have taken the time to describe the world more. It felt slightly as if something was missing. I didn’t get a real feel for the world the characters lived in. This is mainly because the story is too focused on the action and lacks insight delivered in inner reflections by the main character. From another point of view there is no info-dumping. Yeah to that! Instead the information is told in bits and pieces, strewn in almost as an afterthought. <b> Even though the premise is interesting I think the book could have profited from a little bit more reflection or inner monologue. </b> <br /><br />The action is fast paced and thus the book never gets boring. I’ve read it in two days and I am really looking forward to the next in the series. Piper, a Haemon (a cross between human and daemon) wants to become a Consul just like her father. But then the Sahar, an ancient amulet, is stolen and Piper is suspected of the theft. On the run from both the demon hunters and human prefects she can only rely on the help of two demons: Ash and Lyre to uncover the truth behind the attack on the consulate and the whereabouts of her father and her uncle. Their journey leads them from attack to attack and fight to fight. From her home consulate to a hospital, an underground fighting club, an abandoned manor in the woods and some few stops in between. <b>I was really drawn into the story but would have wished for a little bit less fighting and more character interaction.All the fighting felt a little bit repetitive interrupted only by some surprising and some not so surprising twists and turns.</b> It’s here that you see clearly the inexperience of a debut author but one that I am sure in time and with more writing will get masterful in delivering a gripping and fascinating story. <br /><br />What I really loved in this story are the characters and the build-up of the romance. Despite the blurb, there really is no love triangle. Thank God. I loved how the author delivered slowly more and more information about the characters. It was like peeling an onion. Everyone has hidden depths and motives. Some are revealed in this book, some secrets remain to come undone in the future. For me this is exactly the reason to give it 4 instead of 3 stars, because every character here has strengths but also weaknesses. <b>Piper is good fighter, headstrong, with her head on her shoulders. But sometimes she acts rashly and impulsively not thinking everything through and it gets her into bad and dangerous situations.</b> In fact it makes her a really bad consul apprentice as in mediation is clearly not her forte. But also it makes her a good fighter and one who will not so easily give up. She is just the right amount of spunky and fragile and she has humor. I liked her character, a lot. And I’m eagerly waiting to read more about her adventures. <br /><br /><b>In the end it’s a well done coming of age, action oriented urban fantasy with nasty demons, mythological creatures and a spunky heroine. The romance was well developed, leaving room for more in the future. The book reminded me a little bit of the movie Immortal (2004) and Penryn &amp; the End of Days by Susan Ee, although sadly not as dark and freaky. It also reminded me sometimes of The Mortal Instruments by Cassandra Clare with the consulate. </b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18028721818460373903" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1265189527" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer16499314815849576560">Uh oh. Big time what am I going to do now...uh oh. Annette Marie just punched me in the gut and then sucked me into a vortex of crazy with Chase the Dark. Serioulsy. Uh oh.<br/><br/>It's YA and Urban Fantasy. Two of my favorite genres combined. Add in humor, killer writing, boys that make my heart race, a heroine that I actually am rooting for and genuinely like, awesome world-building, and some secrets that are bound to get messy in the next few books and I am hooked.<br/><br/>I'm not even sure how to describe thi</span>
  <span id="freeText16499314815849576560" style="display:none">Uh oh. Big time what am I going to do now...uh oh. Annette Marie just punched me in the gut and then sucked me into a vortex of crazy with Chase the Dark. Serioulsy. Uh oh.<br /><br />It's YA and Urban Fantasy. Two of my favorite genres combined. Add in humor, killer writing, boys that make my heart race, a heroine that I actually am rooting for and genuinely like, awesome world-building, and some secrets that are bound to get messy in the next few books and I am hooked.<br /><br />I'm not even sure how to describe this book without over-explaining or giving away things that I just loved discovering. Sooooo....<br /><br />Oh my gosh, I was a giggly mess while reading this book. Crap. I'm a giggly mess now as I write my convoluted fan-girl review. I love Annette Marie, where oh where has she been all of my reading life. I love the way she writes and her characters and well I am just mad love in love with this series.<br /><br />I'm not even going to bother trying to recount the synopsis or explain what the heck is going on, you can read the synopsis or better yet just go read the book. Now. Pronto. Immediately.<br /><br />Piper is off the hook awesome. Seriously. I love this girl. I want to be besties with this crazy chick. She's bad ass, strong, and willing to go balls to the wall for her family. She has moments were her age shows, but for the most part I just really liked her.<br /><br />Okay...now onto the boys. Crap there I go being all giggly again. Can't wipe the grin from my face over the two, yup! two boys that are in Piper's life and that get dragged into the insanity and rushing fast paced crazy that Piper is sucked into.<br /><br />Lyre and Ash. OMG. Again, where oh where has Annette Marie been all of my reading life. Crap on crackers, the boys...I love them. I'm with Piper on this one, I can't completely decide who I like more.<br /><br />Lyre is a smoking hot Incubus. Just. Wow. Lyre is the bad boy with a golden heart streaking through all of that bad. Fantastically fantastic and fiercely loyal to Ash, his best friend. I loved him, and all of his banter with Piper. He made me grin basically any time he was opening his mouth or teasing the crap out of Piper.<br /><br />And then there's Ash. Oh man. Oh missus. Okay. Maybe I do know who I like more 'cuz my heart just kind of jumps whenever I think about Ash and how he is with Piper. Holy crapazolla.<br /><br />Ash isn't a bad boy. He's just bad. BAD. But oh so good all at the same time. Quietly powerful, he's a Draconian and one of the last of his family line. He's high on the totem pole of badassery and completely intriguing. My goodness. Ash just blew me away. The more I got into this book, the more I wanted to know.<br /><br />And there is this one scene....AH! I can't even. I literally can't even say anything about it, but when you get to that scene between him and Piper....It's a good scene. Really good.<br /><br />Ah!! Okay, so I've fan-girled everywhere.<br /><br />The ending isn't completely frustrating but it definitely leaves you desperately clicking for the next book. Which I've clicked and now I'm off to read! More Piper, Ash &amp; Lyre!!! Eeek!<br /><br />Don't let the YA part of this series scare you off, it doesn't read like YA and for the most part I completely forgot that's what I was reading. But I also love YA...so I digress, but seriously read Chase the Dark, it's amazeballs.<br /><br />Originally posted on <a href="http://www.mmandbooks.com/2015/02/review-chase-dark-by-annette-marie.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Me, Myself &amp; Books</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16499314815849576560" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
